byde whyle haue ſomme trew ſeruaūtis ſhall preche teche people turne hem ſynne thus preyour oure lady god ſparyd take vengeaunce worlde ſo full ſynne curſed leuyng falſe extorcione oppreſſion pore dominua meus et deus meus lord god beleue thou arte verry god man thanne oure lorde ſeyd hym beatiqui crediderunt et non viderunt bleſſed tho beleue ſe thow haſte ſeyn thou beleuiſte yit taryng thomas broughte v ſadder beleue bleſſyng oure lord iheſu criſte thys ſpekyth ſeynte gregori ſeyth thomas ynde thou haſte holpe feythe woldeſte beleue tyll thou haddiſte felyd wounde thanne dyd mary
